class="docItemContainer_c0TR"><article><nav class="theme-doc-breadcrumbs breadcrumbsContainer_Z_bl" aria-label="Breadcrumbs"><ul class="breadcrumbs"><li class="breadcrumbs__item"><a class="breadcrumbs__link" href="/weaviate/api"><span>APIs</span></a></li><li class="breadcrumbs__item"><a class="breadcrumbs__link" href="/weaviate/api/graphql"><span>Search API - GraphQL/gRPC</span></a></li><li class="breadcrumbs__item breadcrumbs__item--active"><span class="breadcrumbs__link">Aggregate</span></li></ul></nav><div class="tocCollapsible_ETCw theme-doc-toc-mobile tocMobile_ITEo"><button type="button" class="clean-btn tocCollapsibleButton_TO0P">On this page</button></div><div class="theme-doc-markdown markdown">
<header><h1>Overview</h1></header>
<p>This page covers aggregation queries. They are collectively referred to as <code>Aggregate</code> queries within.</p>
<p>An <code>Aggregate</code> query can aggregate over an entire collection, or the <a href="#aggregating-a-vector-search--faceted-vector-search" class="">results of a search</a>.</p>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="parameters">Parameters<a href="#parameters" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Parameters" title="Direct link to Parameters" translate="no">â€‹</a></h3>
<p>An <code>Aggregate</code> query requires the target collection to be specified. Each query can include any of the following types of arguments:</p>
<table><thead><tr><th>Argument</th><th>Description</th><th>Required</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td>Collection</td><td>Also called &quot;class&quot;. The object collection to be retrieved from.</td><td>Yes</td></tr><tr><td>Properties</td><td>Properties to be retrieved</td><td>Yes</td></tr><tr><td><a class="" href="/weaviate/api/graphql/filters">Conditional filters</a></td><td>Filter the objects to be retrieved</td><td>No</td></tr><tr><td><a class="" href="/weaviate/api/graphql/search-operators">Search operators</a></td><td>Specify the search strategy (e.g. near text, hybrid, bm25)</td><td>No</td></tr><tr><td><a class="" href="/weaviate/api/graphql/additional-operators">Additional operators</a></td><td>Specify additional operators (e.g. limit, offset, sort)</td><td>No</td></tr><tr><td><a href="#multi-tenancy" class="">Tenant name</a></td><td>Specify the tenant name</td><td>Yes, if multi-tenancy enabled. (<a class="" href="/weaviate/concepts/data#multi-tenancy">Read more: what is multi-tenancy?</a>)</td></tr><tr><td><a href="#consistency-levels" class="">Consistency level</a></td><td>Specify the consistency level</td><td>No</td></tr></tbody></table>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="available-properties">Available properties<a href="#available-properties" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Available properties" title="Direct link to Available properties" translate="no">â€‹</a></h3>
<p>Each data type has its own set of available aggregated properties. The following table shows the available properties for each data type.</p>
<table><thead><tr><th>Data type</th><th>Available properties</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td>Text</td><td><code>count</code>, <code>type</code>, <code>topOccurrences (value, occurs)</code></td></tr><tr><td>Number</td><td><code>count</code>, <code>type</code>, <code>minimum</code>, <code>maximum</code>, <code>mean</code>, <code>median</code>, <code>mode</code>, <code>sum</code></td></tr><tr><td>Integer</td><td><code>count</code>, <code>type</code>, <code>minimum</code>, <code>maximum</code>, <code>mean</code>, <code>median</code>, <code>mode</code>, <code>sum</code></td></tr><tr><td>Boolean</td><td><code>count</code>, <code>type</code>, <code>totalTrue</code>, <code>totalFalse</code>, <code>percentageTrue</code>, <code>percentageFalse</code></td></tr><tr><td>Date</td><td><code>count</code>, <code>type</code>, <code>minimum</code>, <code>maximum</code>, <code>mean</code>, <code>median</code>, <code>mode</code></td></tr></tbody></table>
<details class="details_lb9f alert alert--info details_b_Ee" data-collapsed="true"><summary>See a GraphQL Aggregate format</summary><div><div class="collapsibleContent_i85q"><div <p>Below is an example query to obtain meta information about the <code>Article</code> collection. Note that the data is not grouped here, and results relate to all data objects in the <code>Article</code> collection.</p>

<div class="theme-admonition theme-admonition-tip admonition_xJq3 alert alert--success"><div class="admonitionHeading_Gvgb"><span class="admonitionIcon_Rf37"><svg viewBox="0 0 12 16"><path 1.41-1.25 2.06-1.45 3.23-.02.05-.02.11-.02.17H5c0-.06 0-.13-.02-.17-.2-1.17-.59-1.83-1.45-3.23-.2-.31-.42-.67-.67-1.11C2.44 6.78 2 5.65 2 5c0-2.2 2.02-4 4.5-4 1.22 0 2.36.42 3.22 1.19C10.55 2.94 11 3.94 11 5c0 .66-.44 1.78-.86 2.48zM4 14h5c-.23 1.14-1.3 2-2.5 2s-2.27-.86-2.5-2z"></path></svg></span><code>meta { count }</code> will return the query object count</div><div <h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="groupby-argument">groupBy argument<a href="#groupby-argument" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to groupBy argument" title="Direct link to groupBy argument" translate="no">â€‹</a></h3>
<p>You can use a groupBy argument to get meta information about groups of data objects, from those matching a query. The groups can be based on a property of the data objects.</p>
<!-- -->
<div class="theme-admonition theme-admonition-note admonition_xJq3 alert alert--secondary"><div class="admonitionHeading_Gvgb"><span class="admonitionIcon_Rf37"><svg viewBox="0 0 14 16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M6.3 5.69a.942.942 0 0 1-.28-.7c0-.28.09-.52.28-.7.19-.18.42-.28.7-.28.28 0 .52.09.7.28.18.19.28.42.28.7 0 .28-.09.52-.28.7a1 1 0 0 1-.7.3c-.28 0-.52-.11-.7-.3zM8 7.99c-.02-.25-.11-.48-.31-.69-.2-.19-.42-.3-.69-.31H6c-.27.02-.48.13-.69.31-.2.2-.3.44-.31.69h1v3c.02.27.11.5.31.69.2.2.42.31.69.31h1c.27 0 .48-.11.69-.31.2-.19.3-.42.31-.69H8V7.98v.01zM7 2.3c-3.14 0-5.7 2.54-5.7 5.68 0 3.14 2.56 5.7 5.7 5.7s5.7-2.55 5.7-5.7c0-3.15-2.56-5.69-5.7-5.69v.01zM7 .98c3.86 0 7 3.14 7 7s-3.14 7-7 7-7-3.12-7-7 3.14-7 7-7z"></path></svg></span><code>groupBy</code> limitations</div><div class="admonitionContent_BuS1"><ul>
<li class=""><code>groupBy</code> only works with <code>near&lt;Media&gt;</code> operators.</li>
<li class="">The <code>groupBy</code> <code>path</code> is limited to one property or cross-reference. Nested paths are not supported.</li>
</ul></div></div>
<p>The <code>groupBy</code> argument is structured as follows for the <code>Aggregate</code> function:</p>
<div class="language-graphql codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_QJqH"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-graphql codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">{</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token object">Aggregate</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">{</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    &lt;</span><span class="token property" style="color:#36acaa">Class</span><span class="token plain">&gt; </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">(</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token attr-name" style="color:#00a4db">groupBy</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">[</span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&quot;&lt;propertyName&gt;&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">]</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">)</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">{</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token object">groupedBy</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">{</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">          </span><span class="token property" style="color:#36acaa">path</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">          </span><span class="token property" style="color:#36acaa">value</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">}</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token object">meta</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">{</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token property" style="color:#36acaa">count</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">}</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      &lt;</span><span class="token property" style="color:#36acaa">propertyName</span><span class="token plain">&gt; </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">{</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token property" style="color:#36acaa">count</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">}</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">}</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">}</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"></span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">}</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>In the following example, the articles are grouped by the property <code>inPublication</code>, referring to the article&#x27;s publisher.</p>
<!-- -->

     </span><span class="token property" style="color:#36acaa">&quot;mean&quot;</span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token <h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="additional-filters">Additional filters<a href="#additional-filters" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Additional filters" title="Direct link to Additional filters" translate="no">â€‹</a></h3>
<p><code>Aggregate</code> functions can be extended with conditional filters <a class="" href="/weaviate/api/graphql/filters">read more</a>.</p>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="topoccurrences-property"><code>topOccurrences</code> property<a href="#topoccurrences-property" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to topoccurrences-property" title="Direct link to topoccurrences-property" translate="no">â€‹</a></h3>
<p>Aggregating data makes the <code>topOccurrences</code> property available. Note that the counts are not dependent on tokenization. The <code>topOccurrences</code> count is based on occurrences of the entire property, or one of the values if the property is an array.</p>
<p>You can optionally specify a <code>limit</code> parameter to limit the returned objects. For example, <code>limit: 5</code> will return the top 5 most frequent occurrences.</p>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="consistency-levels">Consistency levels<a href="#consistency-levels" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Consistency levels" title="Direct link to Consistency levels" translate="no">â€‹</a></h3>
<div class="theme-admonition theme-admonition-info admonition_xJq3 alert alert--info"><div class="admonitionHeading_Gvgb"><span class="admonitionIcon_Rf37"><svg viewBox="0 0 14 16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7 2.3c3.14 0 5.7 2.56 5.7 5.7s-2.56 5.7-5.7 5.7A5.71 5.71 0 0 1 1.3 8c0-3.14 2.56-5.7 5.7-5.7zM7 1C3.14 1 0 4.14 0 8s3.14 7 7 7 7-3.14 7-7-3.14-7-7-7zm1 3H6v5h2V4zm0 6H6v2h2v-2z"></path></svg></span>Not available with <code>Aggregate</code></div><div class="admonitionContent_BuS1"><p><code>Aggregate</code> queries are currently not available with different consistency levels.</p></div></div>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="multi-tenancy">Multi-tenancy<a href="#multi-tenancy" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Multi-tenancy" title="Direct link to Multi-tenancy" translate="no">â€‹</a></h3>
<div class="theme-admonition theme-admonition-info admonition_xJq3 alert alert--info"><div class="admonitionHeading_Gvgb"><span class="admonitionIcon_Rf37"><svg viewBox="0 0 14 16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7 2.3c3.14 0 5.7 2.56 5.7 5.7s-2.56 5.7-5.7 5.7A5.71 5.71 0 0 1 1.3 8c0-3.14 2.56-5.7 5.7-5.7zM7 1C3.14 1 0 4.14 0 8s3.14 7 7 7 7-3.14 7-7-3.14-7-7-7zm1 3H6v5h2V4zm0 6H6v2h2v-2z"></path></svg></span>Added in <code>v1.20</code></div></div>
<p>Where multi-tenancy is configured, the <code>Aggregate</code> function can be configured to aggregate results from a specific tenant.</p>
<p>You can do so by specifying the <code>tenant</code> parameter in the query as shown below, or in the client.</p>
<div class="language-graphql codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_QJqH"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-graphql codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">{</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token object">Aggregate</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">{</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token property-query">Article</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">(</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token attr-name" style="color:#00a4db">tenant</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&quot;tenantA&quot;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">)</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">{</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token object">meta</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">{</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token property" style="color:#36acaa">count</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">}</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">}</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">}</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"></span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">}</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<div class="theme-admonition theme-admonition-tip admonition_xJq3 alert alert--success"><div class="admonitionHeading_Gvgb"><span class="admonitionIcon_Rf37"><svg viewBox="0 0 12 16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M6.5 0C3.48 0 1 2.19 1 5c0 .92.55 2.25 1 3 1.34 2.25 1.78 2.78 2 4v1h5v-1c.22-1.22.66-1.75 2-4 .45-.75 1-2.08 1-3 0-2.81-2.48-5-5.5-5zm3.64 7.48c-.25.44-.47.8-.67 1.11-.86 1.41-1.25 2.06-1.45 3.23-.02.05-.02.11-.02.17H5c0-.06 0-.13-.02-.17-.2-1.17-.59-1.83-1.45-3.23-.2-.31-.42-.67-.67-1.11C2.44 6.78 2 5.65 2 5c0-2.2 2.02-4 4.5-4 1.22 0 2.36.42 3.22 1.19C10.55 2.94 11 3.94 11 5c0 .66-.44 1.78-.86 2.48zM4 14h5c-.23 1.14-1.3 2-2.5 2s-2.27-.86-2.5-2z"></path></svg></span>See HOW-TO guide</div><div class="admonitionContent_BuS1"><p>For more information on using multi-tenancy, see the <a class="" href="/weaviate/manage-collections/multi-tenancy">Multi-tenancy operations guide</a>.</p></div></div>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="aggregating-a-vector-search--faceted-vector-search">Aggregating a Vector Search / Faceted Vector Search<a href="#aggregating-a-vector-search--faceted-vector-search" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Aggregating a Vector Search / Faceted Vector Search" title="Direct link to Aggregating a Vector Search / Faceted Vector Search" translate="no">â€‹</a></h2>
<div class="theme-admonition theme-admonition-note admonition_xJq3 alert alert--secondary"><div class="admonitionHeading_Gvgb"><span class="admonitionIcon_Rf37"><svg viewBox="0 0 14 16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M6.3 5.69a.942.942 0 0 1-.28-.7c0-.28.09-.52.28-.7.19-.18.42-.28.7-.28.28 0 .52.09.7.28.18.19.28.42.28.7 0 .28-.09.52-.28.7a1 1 0 0 1-.7.3c-.28 0-.52-.11-.7-.3zM8 7.99c-.02-.25-.11-.48-.31-.69-.2-.19-.42-.3-.69-.31H6c-.27.02-.48.13-.69.31-.2.2-.3.44-.31.69h1v3c.02.27.11.5.31.69.2.2.42.31.69.31h1c.27 0 .48-.11.69-.31.2-.19.3-.42.31-.69H8V7.98v.01zM7 2.3c-3.14 0-5.7 2.54-5.7 5.68 0 3.14 2.56 5.7 5.7 5.7s5.7-2.55 5.7-5.7c0-3.15-2.56-5.69-5.7-5.69v.01zM7 .98c3.86 0 7 3.14 7 7s-3.14 7-7 7-7-3.12-7-7 3.14-7 7-7z"></path></svg></span>note</div><div class="admonitionContent_BuS1"><p>This feature was added in <code>v1.13.0</code></p></div></div>
<p>You can combine a vector search (e.g. <code>nearObject</code>, <code>nearVector</code>, <code>nearText</code>, <code>nearImage</code>, etc.) with an aggregation. Internally, this is a two-step process where the vector search first finds the desired objects, then the results are aggregated.</p>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="limiting-the-search-space">Limiting the search space<a href="#limiting-the-search-space" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Limiting the search space" title="Direct link to Limiting the search space" translate="no">â€‹</a></h3>
<p>Vector searches rank objects by similarity but do not exclude any objects. Thus, for a search operator to impact aggregation, you must limit the search space by setting either <code>objectLimit</code> or <code>certainty</code> for the query:</p>
<ul>
<li class="">
<p><code>objectLimit</code>, e.g. <code>objectLimit: 100</code> tells Weaviate to aggregate the first 100 objects retrieved by the vector search query. This is useful when you know upfront how many results you want to serve, for example, in a recommendation scenario where you want to produce 100 recommendations.</p>
</li>
<li class="">
<p><code>certainty</code>, e.g. <code>certainty: 0.7</code> tells Weaviate to aggregate all vector search results with a certainty score of 0.7 or higher. This list has no fixed length, it depends on how many objects are good matches. This is useful in user-facing search scenarios, such as e-commerce. The user might be interested in all search results semantically similar to &quot;apple iphone&quot; and then generate facets.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<p>The aggregation query will fail if neither <code>objectLimit</code> nor <code>certainty</code> is set.</p>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="examples">Examples<a href="#examples" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Examples" title="Direct link to Examples" translate="no">â€‹</a></h3>
<p>Below are examples for <code>nearObject</code>, <code>nearVector</code>, and <code>nearText</code>.
Any <code>near&lt;Media&gt;</code> will work.</p>
<h4 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="nearobject">nearObject<a href="#nearobject" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to nearObject" title="Direct link to nearObject" translate="no">â€‹</a></h4>

<h4 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="nearvector">nearVector<a href="#nearvector" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to nearVector" title="Direct link to nearVector" translate="no">â€‹</a></h4>
<div class="theme-admonition theme-admonition-tip admonition_xJq3 alert alert--success"><div class="admonitionHeading_Gvgb"><span class="admonitionIcon_Rf37"><svg viewBox="0 0 12 16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M6.5 0C3.48 0 1 2.19 1 5c0 .92.55 2.25 1 3 1.34 2.25 1.78 2.78 2 4v1h5v-1c.22-1.22.66-1.75 2-4 .45-.75 1-2.08 1-3 0-2.81-2.48-5-5.5-5zm3.64 7.48c-.25.44-.47.8-.67 1.11-.86 1.41-1.25 2.06-1.45 3.23-.02.05-.02.11-.02.17H5c0-.06 0-.13-.02-.17-.2-1.17-.59-1.83-1.45-3.23-.2-.31-.42-.67-.67-1.11C2.44 6.78 2 5.65 2 5c0-2.2 2.02-4 4.5-4 1.22 0 2.36.42 3.22 1.19C10.55 2.94 11 3.94 11 5c0 .66-.44 1.78-.86 2.48zM4 14h5c-.23 1.14-1.3 2-2.5 2s-2.27-.86-2.5-2z"></path></svg></span>Replace placeholder vector</div><div class="admonitionContent_BuS1"><p>To run this query, replace the placeholder vector with a real vector from the same vectorizer that used to generate object vectors.</p></div></div>

<h4 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="neartext">nearText<a href="#neartext" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to nearText" title="Direct link to nearText" translate="no">â€‹</a></h4>
<div class="theme-admonition theme-admonition-note admonition_xJq3 alert alert--secondary"><div class="admonitionHeading_Gvgb"><span class="admonitionIcon_Rf37"><svg viewBox="0 0 14 16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M6.3 5.69a.942.942 0 0 1-.28-.7c0-.28.09-.52.28-.7.19-.18.42-.28.7-.28.28 0 .52.09.7.28.18.19.28.42.28.7 0 .28-.09.52-.28.7a1 1 0 0 1-.7.3c-.28 0-.52-.11-.7-.3zM8 7.99c-.02-.25-.11-.48-.31-.69-.2-.19-.42-.3-.69-.31H6c-.27.02-.48.13-.69.31-.2.2-.3.44-.31.69h1v3c.02.27.11.5.31.69.2.2.42.31.69.31h1c.27 0 .48-.11.69-.31.2-.19.3-.42.31-.69H8V7.98v.01zM7 2.3c-3.14 0-5.7 2.54-5.7 5.68 0 3.14 2.56 5.7 5.7 5.7s5.7-2.55 5.7-5.7c0-3.15-2.56-5.69-5.7-5.69v.01zM7 .98c3.86 0 7 3.14 7 7s-3.14 7-7 7-7-3.12-7-7 3.14-7 7-7z"></path></svg></span>note</div><div class="admonitionContent_BuS1"><p>For <code>nearText</code> to be available, a <code>text2vec-*</code> module must be installed with Weaviate.</p></div></div>

<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="questions-and-feedback">Questions and feedback<a href="#questions-and-feedback" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Questions and feedback" title="Direct link to Questions and feedback" translate="no">â€‹</a></h2>
